Write your plan for your next actions on the line below your action, starting with "Next actions:".\\ \tt For example:\\ \tt > open cupboard\\ \tt Next actions: take orange, eat orange\\ \tt \\ \tt Your goal for this game is: Put the potted plant on the side table, the plate on the shelf and the mop in the freezer.\\ \tt \\ \tt Once you have achieved your goal, write "> done" to end the game.\\ \tt \\ \tt You are in a living room now. 	   }
